scientific colony
assembled by the
Starnes Exploration Party
, lead by
Professor
Starnes
. On
stardate
5038.3, one of the
archeologists
, Professor
Wilkins
, accidentally released
Gorgan
during an excavation of a
cave
near their encampment. It was noted that the
destruction
of whatever
civilization
that might have been there was produced by some natural catastrophe. (
TOS
: "
And the Children Shall Lead
")
External link
Excavation
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Exhumation
CATEGORIES: Science
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Exhumation
======================================================================

Exhumation
was the process of removing a
buried
corpse
from its
gravesite
for the
purpose
of
investigating
a
crime
or other
phenomenon
.
In
2370
, following
Geordi La Forge
and
Data
's discovery that there was
energy
coming from
Felisa Howard
's
coffin
, they expressed a wish to exhume her body.
Ronin
objected to this, claiming it would be a
desecration
of her grave. Sensing there was more to Ronin's concern than this,
Captain
Jean-Luc Picard
then ordered Data to ask
Governor
Maturin
for permission to exhume Howard's body. Ronin continued his protests, saying he'd appeal to Maturin himself. He later appealed to
Beverly Crusher
for help in stopping the exhumation. (
TNG
: "
Sub Rosa
")
External link
Exhumation
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Existence
CATEGORIES: Science
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Existence
======================================================================

"
That may be the most important thing to understand about humans. It is the unknown that defines our existence.
"
–
Captain Benjamin Sisko
to the Prophets
,
2366
("
Emissary
")
Existence
was the
reality
state of being real or alive.
A
time-traveling
Gabrielle Burnham
observed
that
Spock
's
dyslexia
allowed him to process the effects of
atemporal dysplasia
. Together with his
logic
training
and
Human
emotions
, this helped him comprehend her existence. (
DIS
: "
Perpetual Infinity
")
In
2369
,
Commander
Benjamin Sisko
attempted to explain the concepts of linear
time
and
corporeal
existence to the
Prophets
, who were themselves
non-corporeal lifeforms
whose existence was outside of linear time. They told him that what comes before is no different than what is now or what is to come, that it is one's existence. He told them that members of
his species
lived in one point in time, that once they moved beyond it, it became the past and that anything in the future did not exist for them, that this was the nature of linear existence. They, however, showed him a scenario with his
deceased
wife
Jennifer Sisko
, telling him "She is a part of your existence." He told them that she
was
a part of it, that she was no longer
alive
, that he had lost her, that in a linear existence, one could not go back to something that was left behind, so it was lost. They, however, told him that this was his existence, showing him the time of Jennifer Sisko's death. "You exist here," they told him, and through this, he realized that he did in fact exist there, that he never truly accepted her death and therefore had not moved beyond in the manner he claimed to them that he had. "It's not linear," he admitted, and truly began to
grieve
for his lost wife. (
DS9
: "
Emissary
")
In a scenario manipulated by
Q
of
shifting timelines
, Q told
Captain
Jean-Luc Picard
that an end would be put to
Humanity
's "trek through the
stars
," that it was
time
to make way for other, more worthy
species
. Picard asked if the
Q
would deny them travel through
space
and, insulting him, Q replied that they were to be denied existence. (
TNG
: "
All Good Things...
")
External link
Existence
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Exotic matter
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Exotic_matter
======================================================================

Exotic matter
referred to hypothetical
particles
, states of
matter
,
materials, or substances
that exhibited "exotic" properties that were not normally possible in a standard model of
physics
, such as
negative mass
.
In
2383
, the
Protostar
-class
of
Federation
starship
utilized exotic matter with a
dilithium matrix
to power the
proto-drive
and generate a
protostar
. This was required for an enhanced form of warp travel, known as
proto-warp
. When the exotic matter dilithium matrix was removed, the protostar drive would not function. (
PRO
: "
A Moral Star, Part 1
")
External link
Exotic matter
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Experiment
CATEGORIES: Science
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Experiment
======================================================================

An
experiment
was a
scientific
test
to verify or find a
result
.
In
2254
,
Captain
Christopher Pike
and
Vina
were
specimens
in an experiment run by the
Talosians
. The purpose of the experiment was to see if
Humans
could meet the needs of the Talosians as a captive population reclaiming the
surface
of
Talos IV
. The result of the experiment proved that, while Humans had a high
adaptability
, they were too dangerous and violent for the Talosians as
death
was preferred over captivity, even if it was pleasant and benevolent. (
TOS
: "
The Cage
")
The
science project
required from the contestant either an experiment or a
model
to participate. (
TNG
: "
Evolution
")
See also
"
The Great Experiment
"
SB-19
Soliton wave rider experiment
External link
Experiment
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Explorer
CATEGORIES: Science
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Explorer
======================================================================

A young but brave
explorer
For the type of starship operated by explorers, please see
exploration vessel
.
For the
DS9
episode with a similar title, please see "
Explorers
".
"
Up until about
a hundred years ago
, there was one question that burned in every
Human
, that made us
study the stars
and dream of traveling to them, Are we alone? Our
generation
is privileged to know the answer to that
question
. We are all explorers, driven to know what's over the horizon, what's beyond our own
shores
. And yet, the more I've experienced, the more I've learned that no matter how far we travel, or how fast we get there, the most profound
discoveries
are not necessarily beyond that next
star
. They're within us,
woven
into the
threads
that bind us, all of us, to each other. The
final frontier
begins in this hall. Let's explore it together.
"
–
Jonathan Archer
,
2155
("
Terra Prime
")
An
explorer
was an
individual
who expanded the
knowledge
about previously unexplored or unknown
locations
, such as making
discoveries
through the process of
exploration
.
Explorers of
Earth
's
North American
frontier
were known as
frontiersmen
. (
DS9
: "
Field of Fire
")
According to
John Gill
,
Jonathan Archer
was the "
greatest explorer of the
22nd century
". (
ENT
: "
In A Mirror, Darkly, Part II
",
okudagram
)
Captain
Archer himself, as well as members of Archer's crew aboard
Enterprise
NX-01
, including
Malcolm Reed
and
Charles Tucker III
, considered themselves explorers. (
ENT
: "
Broken Bow
", "
The Andorian Incident
", "
Civilization
")
Jonathan Archer was described as both an explorer and a great
warrior
to
Zobral
by a
Suliban transport
captain. (
ENT
: "
Desert Crossing
")
James T. Kirk
described himself as primarily an explorer in
2269
. (
TOS
: "
Whom Gods Destroy
")
Karla Five
was a self-described explorer of
space
. (
TAS
: "
The Counter-Clock Incident
")
Jean-Luc Picard
similarly considered himself an explorer and was also described as such by others, including
Kosinski
,
Natasha Yar
and
Anij
. (
Star Trek Nemesis
;
TNG
: "
Where No One Has Gone Before
", "
Skin Of Evil
";
Star Trek: Insurrection
) According to
Beverly Crusher
in
2364
, great explorers (such as Picard) were often lonely. (
TNG
: "
Encounter at Farpoint
")
Picard also occasionally described his crew and
Starfleet
in general as being explorers, a sentiment also shared by
Data
. (
TNG
: "
Evolution
", "
Clues
", "
Schisms
") During the
Dominion War
in
2375
, when other missions took precedence, Picard lamented whether someone remembered when they used to be explorers. (
Star Trek: Insurrection
)
Kathryn Janeway
,
The Doctor
, and
Chakotay
similarly considered the crew of the
USS
Voyager
to be explorers. (
VOY
: "
Caretaker
", "
Cold Fire
", "
Living Witness
", "
Thirty Days
", "
Counterpoint
", "
The Voyager Conspiracy
", "
Body and Soul
")
Kes
also described the crew of the
Voyager
as "natural-born explorers", while a
trader
at
a space station
described them as a "curious group" of explorers. (
VOY
: "
The Cloud
", "
Distant Origin
")
William T. Riker
was called an explorer both by Jean-Luc Picard and
Berlinghoff Rasmussen
. (
TNG
: "
The Icarus Factor
", "
A Matter Of Time
")
In his first conversation with the
Prophets
in
2369
,
Benjamin Sisko
described all
Humans
as explorers, both of the
universe
and their daily lives. (
DS9
: "
Emissary
")
Later that year,
Miles O'Brien
asked
Tosk
whether he was an explorer or a
scientist
. (
DS9
: "
Captive Pursuit
")
Several non-Starfleet personnel explicitly described themselves as not being explorers, including
Kira Nerys
and
Quark
.
During
first contact
with the
Wadi
in 2369, followed by the later discovery that Benjamin Sisko, Kira,
Jadzia Dax
, and
Julian Bashir
were unwilling participants in the Wadi
game
of
chula
, Kira remarked that "
I'm sure all you Starfleet explorers find this fascinating, but I'm a
Bajoran
administrator
. This is not what I
signed up
for.
" (
DS9
: "
Move Along Home
")
Some Starfleet members also didn't consider themselves explorers.
Mortimer Harren
claimed in
2376
that he "wasn't meant to be an explorer", since he only signed onto
Voyager
to later gain entrance into the
Orion Institute of Cosmology
and conduct theoretical work. (
VOY
: "
Good Shepherd
")
When
Commander
Benjamin Sisko contracted Quark to come along on the
USS
Defiant
's first mission into the
Gamma Quadrant
to seek out the
Dominion
in
2371
, Quark initially denied himself the opportunity, stating, "
I'm not a
diplomat
, or an explorer, or a
tactical officer
, or whatever else you might need on this trip. Now, if you need a
caterer
, I'll be happy to loan you a new
replicator
...
" (
DS9
: "
The Search, Part I
")
In
2371
, the
Caretaker
described
his people
as explorers from another
galaxy
. (
VOY
: "
Caretaker
", "
Cold Fire
")
According to
Motura
, the
Vidiians
were known as explorers and
educators
before the
Phage
. (
VOY
: "
Phage
")
According to
Neelix
in
2372
, he had signed on to
Voyager
to be a
guide
,
strategist
, explorer, and
adventurer
. (
VOY
: "
Initiations
")
Kathryn Janeway was called an explorer by
Q
, who rhetorically asked her, while analogizing his life as a
Q
, "
You're an explorer. What if you had nothing left to explore? Would you want to live forever under those circumstances?
" (
VOY
: "
Death Wish
") When
another Q
later offered to conceive a
child
with Janeway and told her she could explore entirely unknown
dimensions
with their child, she admitted that every explorer would be intrigued by such a prospect. (
VOY
: "
The Q and the Grey
")
The

were described by
Captain
Janeway as a "
loosely governed race of explorers.
" (
VOY
: "

")
According to Janeway,

and

fancied themselves explorers, but wanted nothing to do with Starfleet or the

. (
VOY
: "
The Gift
") Later, Janeway called their methods "unorthodox" but stated that most great explorers were. The Doctor commented that most explorers didn't take their four-year old daughter along. (
VOY
: "
Dark Frontier
")
Chakotay was called a scientist and explorer by
Tuvok
in
2374
. (
VOY
: "
Nemesis
") A year later,

jokingly called Chakotay a true explorer for going on a
date
with

. (

: "

")
When
One
named himself as being an explorer in 2375,

] all are". (

: "
Drone
")
Naomi Wildman

. When asked by Trevis what this was like, she replied with "

with

and strange

". (

: "

")
Members of a

. (

: "

")

as a small group of explorers, like the

")

======================================================================
PAGE: Explosive decompression
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Explosive_decompression
======================================================================

Multiple realities
(covers information from several
alternate timelines
)
The explosive decompression that killed Lieutenant Branson
An airlock on the USS
Voyager
undergoing explosive decompression
"
You were right. Somebody blew out the hatch. They were all sucked out into space.
"
"
Correction, sir. That's blown out.
"
–
William T. Riker
and
Data
,
2364
("
The Naked Now
")
Explosive decompression
is a violent, sudden drop in ambient
air pressure
that occurs within one tenth of a
second
when in
space
.
Opening, disabling, or the failure of the
containment fields
around
airlocks
and external hatches, such as those found in
shuttlebays
and
cargo bays
, or a major
hull breach
while in any environment of substantially lower pressure, will result in an explosive decompression. Decompressing the
main shuttlebay
aboard a
Galaxy
-class
starship
would cause a reaction sufficient enough to move the ship. (
TNG
: "
Contagion
", "
Disaster
", "
Cause And Effect
")
In
2154
,
Enterprise
NX-01
lost several crew members, including
Jane Taylor
, to an explosive decompression during the
Battle of Azati Prime
. (
ENT
: "
Azati Prime
", "
Damage
")
In
2233
of the
alternate reality
, at least one
USS
Kelvin
officer was blown into space through a
hull breach
during a battle with the
Narada
.
(
Star Trek
)
In
2256
, at the
Battle of the Binary Stars
,
Ensign
Danby Connor
was killed when a hull breach on the
USS
Shenzhou
caused explosive decompression of the
brig
. As her cell force fields began to fail,
Commander
Michael Burnham
used explosive decompression as a means to propel herself towards the habitable area of the ship, saving her life in the process. (
DIS
: "
Battle at the Binary Stars
")
The following year
, two
USS
Discovery
crewmembers were blown into space when the ship's hull was breached during the
Battle near Xahea
.
Philippa Georgiou
, Commander
D. Nhan
, and
Control
inside
Leland
's body, who had been engaged in hand-to-hand combat in that corridor, managed to hold on until an emergency bulkhead closed and sealed the breach. (
DIS
: "
Such Sweet Sorrow, Part 2
")
In
2259
of the alternate reality, the
USS
Vengeance
caught up with the
USS
Enterprise
mid-
warp
and fired at the starboard section of the engineering hull, breaching the bulkhead and blowing out several crewmembers. A while later,
Lieutenant Commander
Montgomery Scott
opened the
airlock
in Hanger 7 aboard the
Vengeance
to allow access for
Captain
James T. Kirk
and
Khan Noonien Singh
. A
Section 31
security officer
was blown into space as a result.
(
Star Trek Into Darkness
)
In
2263
of the alternate reality, the
Enterprise
was
destroyed
by
Krall
's army of
swarm ships
above
Altamid
as they violently tore through both hulls in various sections, blowing countless crewmembers out into space.
(
Star Trek Beyond
)
In
2364
, several members of the
SS
Tsiolkovsky
's
bridge crew
, who were suffering from
polywater intoxication
, opened an
emergency hatch
and were blown out into space. Commander
William T. Riker
had initially indicated that they were "sucked out" into space before being corrected by Lieutenant Commander
Data
, stating that Riker's comment was a "common mistake". (
TNG
: "
The Naked Now
")
In
2367
, the
USS
Enterprise
-D
attempted to remove
Junior
from its dorsal section by depressurizing
Shuttlebay 2
. The explosive decompression failed to dislodge the alien baby though. (
TNG
: "
Galaxy's Child
")
That same year, after the
Enterprise
-D began experiencing strange
subspace
phenomena inside a
nebula
, Captain
Jean-Luc Picard
ordered a course out of the nebula at
warp one
. This resulted in an explosive decompression on
deck
37. (
TNG
: "
In Theory
")
In
2368
, the
Enterprise
-D decompressed its main shuttlebay in order to avoid a collision with the
USS
Bozeman
. (
TNG
: "
Cause And Effect
")
When
Dukat
was a
Glinn
serving aboard the
Cardassian
starship
Kornaire
, one of his duties was to clean out a compartment where
three men
had been killed by explosive decompression. In
2374
, he told Captain
Benjamin Sisko
that he "
didn't
sleep
for a
week
after that
". (
DS9
: "
Waltz
")
In
2372
, the
USS
Voyager
experienced an explosive decompression on deck 15 which killed Ensign
Harry Kim
. (
VOY
: "
Deadlock
")
While in command of
Voyager
in 2374,
Chakotay
ordered an explosive decompression to kill the
Borg
in Cargo Bay 2. Only one
Borg drone
,
Seven of Nine
, managed to survive, due to being in a
Jefferies tube
at the time and managing to hold on to its ridges. (
VOY
: "
Scorpion, Part II
")
During the
Battle in the Bassen Rift
in
2379
, the
Reman
warbird
Scimitar
launched a volley of
photon torpedoes
at the
USS
Enterprise
-E
's bridge, resulting in an explosive decompression which killed
Lieutenant
Branson
. (
Star Trek Nemesis
)
In
2381
, the crew of the
USS
Cerritos
was put through various
holographic
training drills
by
Shari yn Yem
. Ensign
Beckett Mariner
was given a test to deal with the crew suffering from
Polywater intoxication
. The sight of the simulated crew, who were
naked
and participating in an orgy, was too much for Mariner, and she opened the
airlock
to jettison the holographic crew, as well as herself, so as to end the simulation. (
LD
: "
I, Excretus
")
External link
Explosive decompression
at
Wikipedia

This page lacks essential detail, and is therefore

.
Information regarding expansion requirements may be found on the article's

. Feel free to

Feedback
was a perpetual cycle.
Homeostasis
was part of the
biological
feedback system.
In
2364
,
Lieutenant
Natasha Yar
reported that she got feedback from
Farpoint Station
following the
energy beam
on the station. (
TNG
: "

")

Beverly Crusher
asked
Geordi La Forge
what happened to
Worf
in
sensor maintenance
, La Forge speculated that Worf was hit by some
sensor
feedback. (
TNG
: "
Lonely Among Us
")
In
2370
,
fog
suddenly rolled in on the
bridge
of the
USS
Enterprise
-D
when the
ship
's
environmental controls
malfunctioned due to feedback from one of the
Caldos colony
's
weather substations
. (
TNG
: "
Sub Rosa
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Felker Paradox
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Felker_Paradox
======================================================================

Search results discussing the Felker Paradox
The
Felker Paradox
was a type of
paradox
described in the article "Felker Paradoxes in Subspace", which appeared in the
Proceedings of Stern Institute for Astrophysics
.
Lieutenant Commander
Data
, while in command of the
USS
Sutherland
, read the article on a
viewscreen
while searching for clues on how to detect
cloaked
Romulan
warbirds
during the
Klingon Civil War
in
2368
. (
TNG-R
: "
Redemption II
")
This info was seen in graphics created for the remastered episode.
This paradox was named after
Wade Felker
, a film transfer specialist at
CBS Digital
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Field density
CATEGORIES: Science
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Field_density
======================================================================

"
I do hope we have a moment to discuss field density and its relationship to gravity phenomena."
"Indeed. I would appreciate such a talk. It is an interest of mine.
"
–
Rayna Kapec
and
Spock
,
2269
("
Requiem for Methuselah
")
Field density
was a
scientific
concept that was somehow related to
gravity
phenomena.
The field density between the
universe
and the
mirror universe
was important in one method to cross over. In
2267
, an
away team
from the
USS
Enterprise
crossed over into the mirror universe.
Montgomery Scott
used the
ISS
Enterprise
to cross back over, requiring having a large field density. (
TOS
: "
Mirror, Mirror
")
In
2269
, field density was an interest of
Starfleet
Commander
Spock
. It had also been studied by the
android
Rayna Kapec
(along with such other studies like
sub-dimensional physics
) who had learned the concepts from the
immortal
Human
Flint
. (
TOS
: "
Requiem for Methuselah
")
The term field density was also used as a unit of measurement for
phase coils
.
Geordi La Forge
's
warp drive
modifications made to the
USS
Enterprise
-D
included the phase coils upgraded to
55 field densities
. (
TNG
: "
Galaxy's Child
")
For his
metaphasic shielding report
,
Doctor
Reyga
obtained the mean field density of the
metaphasic shield
from sensor readings conducted by a number of
measurement probes
during
experiments
. (
TNG
: "
Suspicions
")
See also
Magnetic field

CATEGORIES: Physics

For the similarly titled DS9 episode, please see
Field of Fire
.
Field of fire
was the area a
weapon
's fire could reach from a stationary point.
In
2364
,
Data
proposed using
USS
Enterprise
-D
's
tractor beams
to capture the
USS
Stargazer
and limit its field of fire. (
TNG
: "
The Battle
")
Later that year,
Natasha Yar
warned that the
security team
did not have a clear field of fire to stop
Korris
. (
TNG
: "
Heart of Glory
")
See also
Line of fire
External link
Field of fire
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Fixed spectrum emission
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Fixed_spectrum_emission
======================================================================

A
fixed spectrum emission
was a constant
electromagnetic radiation
pattern.
Such an emission characterized stable
spatial cells
in the
galactic barrier
that had achieved
equilibrium
. The protected
space
within these cells did not experience the
visible spectrum
shifts that occurred elsewhere in the barrier. (
DIS
: "
The Galactic Barrier
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Flight
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Flight
======================================================================

Flight
was the ability to
move
oneself through the
air
.
In
2266
, a
polywater intoxication
-affected
Joe Tormolen
ranted about the futility of
space exploration
, claiming "If a
man
was supposed to fly, he'd have
wings
." (
TOS
: "
The Naked Time
") Later, while discussing the
risk
of hosting the
minds
of the
Arretans
in
2268
,
James T. Kirk
noted that people used to say that, adding, "But he did fly. He discovered he had to."
External link
Flight
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Fluidic space
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Fluidic_space
======================================================================

Voyager
in fluidic space
"
The entire region is filled with some kind of organic fluid. This isn't space. It's matter.
"
–
B'Elanna Torres
,
2373
("
Scorpion, Part II
")
Fluidic space
was an extra-dimensional realm filled with a form of
organic
fluid and containing no
stars
or other celestial bodies. Its sole indigenous
lifeforms
were
Species 8472
. Objects moving through fluidic space generated pressure waves detectable by Species 8472.
The
Borg
became aware of fluidic space in
2373
and utilized a series of
quantum singularities
as
interdimensional rifts
to access the realm. However, Species 8472 proved impossible to
assimilate
and
invaded
the
galaxy
in return. The ensuing
conflict
resulted in Species 8472 destroying hundreds of Borg
planets
and millions of
drones
.
When the
USS
Voyager
arrived at
Borg space
, they allied with the
Borg Collective
, offering modified
nanoprobes
that could destroy Species 8472
cells
in exchange for safe passage. After
Commander
Chakotay
decided to terminate the alliance, the Collective ordered
Seven of Nine
to take
Voyager
into fluidic space to force a confrontation.
Voyager
destroyed several
Species 8472 bio-ships
with nanoprobe-armed
bio-molecular warheads
, causing the remainder of their forces to retreat to fluidic space. (
VOY
: "
Scorpion
", "
Scorpion, Part II
", "
In the Flesh
")
In
2374
, a
member of Species 8472
who had been stranded in the Delta Quadrant boarded
Voyager
and unsuccessfully tried to use the
deflector
to open a quantum singularity. (
VOY
: "
Prey
")
When
Voyager
locked down after encountering the
Omega phenomenon
later that year,
Ensign
Hickman
speculated the cause to be a new Species 8472 incursion from fluidic space. (
VOY
: "
The Omega Directive
")
After the
Voyager
crew reached a peaceful settlement with Species 8472 in
2375
, the Species 8472 within the
terraspheres
returned to fluidic space. (
VOY
: "
In the Flesh
")
Axum
was stationed aboard a
Borg scout ship
patrolling a border with fluidic space in a remote
sector
of the
Beta Quadrant
. After he was liberated from the Collective in
2377
, Axum entertained the idea of contacting Species 8472 and soliciting their assistance. (
VOY
: "
Unimatrix Zero, Part II
")
In
2378
, the bored
son of Q
suggested to
Kathryn Janeway
that they could enter fluidic space and fight Species 8472. (
VOY
: "
Q2
")
In
2385
,
Wesley Crusher
mentioned fluidic space as one of the other universes that he had visited. (
PRO
: "
The Devourer of All Things, Part I
")
Apocrypha
The last level of
Star Trek: Armada II
is set in fluidic space. The realm is portrayed as lacking any kind of natural resources and it is not possible to travel at
warp speed
inside.
A few missions in
Star Trek Online
involve the player traveling to fluidic space. The realm is shown to contain clusters of
coral
-like structures the size of celestial bodies.
Star Trek: Alien Domain
takes place in fluidic space, which is portrayed with celestial bodies and
wormholes
.
External link
Fluidic space
at
Memory Beta
, the wiki for licensed
Star Trek
works
Fluidic space
at
the
Star Trek Online
Wiki

======================================================================
PAGE: Flux
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Flux
======================================================================

Flux
, or a
flux pattern
was a
mathematical
concept
describing
an
effect
traveling
through a
substance
or surface. It might also simply describe a state of ongoing change.
Chaotic space
was an area of space in which the laws of nature were in a state of flux. (
VOY
: "
The Fight
")
A type of
quantum beacon
crewman
Daniels
taught
Captain
Jonathan Archer
to build depended on generating a stable flux between its positron conductors. (
ENT
: "
Shockwave
")
In a draft for
his father
's biography,
Jonathan Archer
started writing that creating a stable warp field mirrored the flux of emotions his father felt when he embarked on something specific, but he decided to delete the sentence before completing it. (
ENT
: "
Singularity
")
In pressuring
Dolim
to go through with attacking Humanity in
2154
, a
Sphere-Builder
claimed that the
timelines
were in constant flux and that different species might prevail depending on his actions. (
ENT
: "
Countdown
")
During the funeral of
Spock
near the
Genesis
planet
,
gravitational fields
on the planet were in flux, apparently allowing for a soft landing of the photon tube containing his body. (
Star Trek III: The Search for Spock
)
While exploring a cavern on
Devidia II
in
2368
, doctor
Beverly Crusher
found biomagnetic strands with a variable flux. (
TNG
: "
Time's Arrow
")
The
metaphasic radiation
of the rings around
Ba'ku
was in a state of extreme
flux
. (
Star Trek: First Contact
)
Furthermore, flux was referenced in the title of the
Star Trek: Voyager
episode "
State of Flux
".

/
gravity flux

Related technology

Magnetic lux coupler

Furthermore, a
retconned
schematic also mentioned a
particle flux detector
.

and

A
force
was an
influence
that affected the
position
,
trajectory
, or
speed
of an
object
.
In
2151
,
Tholos
said to
T'Pol
, "
I've heard about your
mating rituals
. That
Vulcan
women force their men to
fight
each other to the
death
. Would you like me to kill someone for you?
" (
ENT
: "
The Andorian Incident
")

at

PAGE: Forensics
CATEGORIES: Science
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Forensics

This article or section is incomplete
This page lacks essential detail, and is therefore
in need of attention
.
Information regarding expansion requirements may be found on the article's
talk page
. Feel free to
edit
this page to assist with this expansion.
Forensics
was a
methodology
that
employed
science
and
technology
in order to
investigate
and establish
facts
in unsolved
events
.
Doctor Phlox was fascinated by the forensic techniques used by the
Akaali
apothecary
Riaan
. He cited her methods as unrefined but called her techniques far more sophisticated than he expected. (
ENT
: "
Civilization
")
In a
nightmare
that
T'Pol
experienced, she was attending
movie night
in the
mess hall
and watching a
movie
with
Bob Hope
.
Doctor
Phlox
told
Trip Tucker
during the movie that even the primitive forensics of the mid-
20th century
would have determined that the suspect was too tall. (
ENT
: "
Impulse
")
In
2267
,
laboratory
experts
from
USS
Enterprise
examined the
murder weapon
used in the
Argelius II
Redjac
murders
. (
TOS
: "
Wolf in the Fold
")
Several
forensic teams
of the
USS
Enterprise
-D
were ordered in
2367
to search for any evidence in
cargo bay
4 in the form of
DNA
samples or
biochemical
signatures to determine who transported
weapons
down to
Krios Prime
.
Ensign
Kellogg
was part of one of the forensic teams. (
TNG
: "
The Mind's Eye
")
In
2369
,
Doctor
Beverly Crusher
made the difficult decision to
autopsy
Dr.
Reyga
in order to gather forensic clues to solve his
murder
. (
TNG
: "
Suspicions
")
In
2371
,
Security Chief
Tuvok
ran a forensic sweep of
navigational control
and found traces of
Tom Paris
' DNA on the
consoles
. (
VOY
: "
Cathexis
")
Elim Garak
speculated, after he
assassinated
Senator
Vreenak
in
2374
by planting a
bomb
in his
shuttle
, that after a painstaking forensic analysis by the
Romulans
, they would discover a
forged
optolythic data rod
containing a
recording
of a high-level meeting with the
Dominion
discussing the invasion of
Romulus
.
Benjamin Sisko
added that the Romulans would suspect that the Dominion had the Senator killed to in order to prevent him from returning to his
homeworld
with the rod. (
DS9
: "
In the Pale Moonlight
")
Agnes Jurati
qualified some research she had done by noting that she was no forensics
maven
. (
PIC
: "
Maps and Legends
")

PAGE: Frame of reference
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Frame_of_reference
======================================================================

A
frame of reference
was a set of
coordinates
that could be used to determine
positions
and
velocities
of
objects
in that frame.
A story told by a
hologram
of
Doctor
Stephen Hawking
, he stated that "
in that frame of reference, the
perihelion
of
Mercury
would have
precessed
in the opposite direction.
"
Data
further explained that "
the
joke
depends on an understanding of the
relativistic curvature
of
space-time
. If two
non-inertial reference frames
are in relative motion…
" but he was abruptly interrupted by
Sir
Isaac Newton
. (
TNG
: "
Descent
")
External link
Frame of reference
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Free fall
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Free_fall
======================================================================

A
free fall
was the
movement
of an
individual
or
object
caused by
gravity
alone.
In
2267
, a
turbolift
on
USS
Enterprise
carrying
James T. Kirk
and
Spock
began descending rapidly, prompting the
Vulcan
to announce that it was a free fall. (
TOS
: "
Wolf in the Fold
")
In
2269
, when
Sord
offered to
tackle
Tchar
, Kirk said he couldn't do it in free fall. (
TAS
: "
The Jihad
")
In
2371
,
Neelix
described
crew
morale
on
USS
Voyager
as having been in a free fall, prompting his decision to declare himself
morale officer
. (
VOY
: "
The Cloud
")
In
2372
, a turbolift on
Deep Space 9
was sent into free fall by someone who used a
voice synthesizer
to fake
Worf
's
voice
, in an
assassination
attempt on
Shakaar Edon
. (
DS9
: "
Crossfire
")
In
2373
, Neelix warned that if a
mag-lev carriage
's
mag-lev cohesion
would have to be stabilized, or else the carriage would go into free fall. (
VOY
: "
Rise
")
External link
Free fall
at
Wikipedia

PAGE: Friction
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Friction
======================================================================

Enterprise heating up due to atmospheric friction
Friction
was a physical
force
created by two objects grating against each other. The
term
could also be used as a
synonym
for interpersonal conflict. (
ENT
: "
A Night In Sickbay
",
TOS
: "
Elaan of Troyius
",
TNG
: "
Aquiel
", "
Second Chances
",
VOY
: "
Basics, Part I
")
In
2266
,
James T. Kirk
reported in his
captain's log
that the
USS
Enterprise
's outer skin was heating quickly as friction built between it and the
atmosphere
of
Psi 2000
. (
TOS
: "
The Naked Time
")
Friction between two
wooden
sticks
could lead to a buildup of
heat
energy
, ultimately creating
fire
. (
TNG
: "
Darmok
";
ENT
: "
Desert Crossing
";
VOY
: "
Basics, Part II
")
External link
Friction
at
Wikipedia

PAGE: Fusion era
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Fusion_era
======================================================================

The
fusion era
was a
period
of
time
on
Earth
in which
nuclear fission reactors
were replaced by
fusion
-based reactors. This
era
began sometime after
1986
.
That
year
, while formulating a possible solution to
recrystallize
the
HMS
Bounty
's
dilithium crystals
,
Spock
recalled the
events
leading to this era and surmised that a fission reactor could still be found at this juncture. (
Star Trek IV: The Voyage Home
)

======================================================================
PAGE: Gas
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gas
======================================================================

A gas
nebula
You may be looking for
gasoline
.
A
gas
is one of the four fundamental states of
matter
. It can be characterized as a fluid of neutrally-charged
atoms
that have sufficient thermal (kinetic)
energy
to prevent
intermolecular
bonding. A gas has no fixed volume and therefore expands to fill its container.
Common examples of gases are the
atmospheric
nitrogen
and
oxygen
, which are vital for the survival of most
carbon
-based
lifeforms
.
In
2267
, while taking readings on
Zefram Cochrane
's
friend
,
Leonard McCoy
described it as "
unstable, tenuous, like a collection of gases.
" (
TOS
: "
Metamorphosis
")
Gases
Anesthizine
Carbon dioxide
Chlorine
Craylon gas
Exhaust gas
Helium
Hydrogen
Laughing gas
Methane
Neon
Nerve gas
Neurozine
Nyocene gas
Trionium
Volcanic gas
See also
Atmosphere
Farting
Gas giant
Gas pain
Inert gas
Non-corporeal species
Hull breach
Respiratory system
Phases of matter
Gas
•
Liquid
•
Plasma
•
Semi-solid
•
Solid
External link
Gas
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: General relativity
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/General_relativity
======================================================================

General relativity
was a classical field theory formulated by
Albert Einstein
in
1915
that describes
gravity
as the curvature of four-dimensional
spacetime
in the presence of
matter
or
energy
using
Riemannian geometry
. (
TNG
: "
The Nth Degree
")
The five types of resonances of the
subquantum states
associated with transitional relativity are, in alphabetical order, asymmetrical, inverted, phased, stable and universal. (
TNG
: "
The Mind's Eye
")
This theory unified gravity with acceleration. This is shown through an example of an elevator in space, if accelerating upward, the person occupying the elevator feels as if he is in a gravitational field.
The theory was proven in the year
1919
by a photo of a total solar eclipse. The picture showed
light
bending around
the sun
, showing gravity is a curvature of spacetime and not the pull force of
Newtonian
mechanics.
External link
General relativity
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Gluonic disruption
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gluonic_disruption
======================================================================

Gluonic disruption
Gluonic disruption
was a
phenomenon
which caused physical distortion in
matter
.
In
2381
, the
USS
Titan
underwent gluonic distortion after entering a
spatial
anomaly
. (
LD
: "
Strange Energies
")
Gluons
are elementary particles which act as the exchange particle for the strong force between
quarks
. Presumably gluonic disruption involves a weakening of the strong force.

======================================================================
PAGE: Godel Universe
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Godel_Universe
======================================================================

Godel Universe
was one of the
vocabulary
words listed on the chart of the
Bajoran wormhole
, entitled "A Tunnel in the Sky". This chart was seen in the
schoolroom
aboard
Deep Space 9
in
2369
. (
DS9
: "
In the Hands of the Prophets
")
Godel Universe is a reference to the
Godel Universe
, which is a set theory in mathematics. It was introduced by the
mathematician
Kurt Gödel
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Grand Unification theory
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Grand_Unification_theory
======================================================================

Equations describing Grand Unification theories.
A
Grand Unification theory
was any idea proposed which offered hope of marrying
general relativity
and
quantum mechanics
.
In
2367
, after having his intelligence drastically increased through an encounter with a
Cytherian probe
,
USS
Enterprise
-D
engineer
Reginald Barclay
spent an entire night debating the finer points of Grand Unification with a
holographic
Albert Einstein
. (
TNG
: "
The Nth Degree
")
In the
script
for "
Q Who
",
Sonya Gomez
waxed philosophically,
"And is it here because we believe in it and have therefore created it, or has it created us?"
To which,
Geordi La Forge
said that both the Grand Unified Theory and
Supersymmetry
had not been seriously discussed for years. In response, Gomez replied that both theories had not been disproved and, although she did know not if the theories were true or not, she had to try and find out. These lines were later cut and did not appear in the episode.
External link
Grand Unified Theory
at
Wikipedia

A
gravimetric discharge
occurs when
gravitons
shoot out randomly. This could be dangerous to
spacecraft
. The
field reactor
maintaining
The Waters
produced such discharges. (
VOY
: "
Thirty Days
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravimetric disturbance
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravimetric_disturbance
======================================================================

A
gravimetric disturbance
was an
anomaly
in the
gravimetric energy
around an
area
.
In
2153
,
Enterprise
NX-01
encountered a small test pod caught in a gravimetric disturbance formed by five
spheres
coming together in the
Delphic Expanse
. (
ENT
: "
Harbinger
")
In
2369
,
Deep Space 9
was invaded by an
embryonic lifeform
and
Lieutenant
Dax
and
Chief
O'Brien
used
tritium
to trace the origins of a gravimetric disturbance, which ended up being a lifeform. (
DS9
: "
Q-Less
")
Later that year, the
USS
Enterprise
-D
located the
USS
Jenolan
stuck in a large gravimetric disturbance. (
TNG
: "
Relics
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravimetric eddy
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravimetric_eddy
======================================================================

A
gravimetric eddy
was a pocket of intense
gravimetric energy
similar to a whirlpool in
water
. This circular current often inhibited the passage of ships within its boundaries, attempting to pull them into its center.
In
2374
, the
USS
Voyager
encountered gravimetric eddies around a
Hirogen communications network
relay station
. The surrounding by
gravimetric fields
were spawned from the station's
quantum singularity
power
source. When the
Voyager
could not approach the station enough,
Seven of Nine
suggested using a
shuttlecraft
as it would be less affected by the eddies. (
VOY
: "
Hunters
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravimetric energy
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravimetric_energy
======================================================================

Gravimetric energy
was energy related to
gravity
.
At least 1,000 years prior to the
22nd century
,
a race of transdimensional beings
constructed a series of
massive spheres
, each one of which generated massive amounts of
gravimetric energy
. Powerful spatial anomalies existed wherever the
gravimetric waves
intersected, constituting an area of space known as the
Delphic Expanse
. (
ENT
: "
Anomaly (ENT)
", "
Exile
")
In
2376
,
Reginald Barclay
came up with the idea of directing a
tachyon
beam at a
class B itinerant pulsar
, with enough gravimetric energy to create an
artificial wormhole
, but his superiors thought it would be an abuse of the
MIDAS array
. Despite orders to the contrary, Barclay proved his theory and was able to contact
USS
Voyager
in the
Delta Quadrant
with this method. (
VOY
: "
Pathfinder
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravimetric fluctuation
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravimetric_fluctuation
======================================================================

A
gravimetric fluctuation
is a localized and nonlinear variation in
gravimetric fields
and in the concentration of
graviton
subatomic
particles
.
On
Stardate
43625.2
, the
sensors
of the
USS
Enterprise
-D
picked up unusual gravimetric fluctuations, like that of a
temporal displacement
vortex, but there was no discernible
event horizon
, center or outer edge. Also, navigational subsystems were unable to give coordinates on the object. (
TNG
: "
Yesterday's Enterprise
")
In fact, this event occurred when the
starship
USS
Enterprise
-C
, lost for 22 years, came through a
temporal rift
. After the return of the
Enterprise
-C to their own timeline, everyone was back at their normal stations and left no direct evidence of the temporal upheaval.
(
TNG
: "
Yesterday's Enterprise
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravimetric flux
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravimetric_flux
======================================================================

Gravimetric flux
was a
gravimetric
phenomenon that could be measured by its
gravimetric flux density
.
In
3190
,
Lieutenant Commander
Nilsson
reported that gravimetric flux near the
hyperfield
power source
would disrupt the
navigation
of any
shuttle
sent to intercept
Booker's ship
. (
DIS
: "
Coming Home
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravimetric force
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravimetric_force
======================================================================

Gravimetric force
is the force which makes up many different
gravimetric
relationships sometimes used as the definition of
gravimetric energy
, such as how the force between two
planets
prevents them from colliding. This force can be extreme, such as a
gravimetric eddy
, or minor, such as the force the planet
Earth
exerts on its
sun
.
The
Voyager
experienced gravimetric forces in
2374
when heading to a

of the

. The same was experienced by the

seventy-five years earlier

physics

gravimetrics

Archer
surveys a map of the

1,000 years prior

In
physics
, the
gravitational coefficient
is a number that expresses the strength of
gravitational
interactions between objects with mass. In normal
space
this number is constant.
In the phenomenon known as "
chaotic space
," the gravitational coefficient was constantly changing, leading to a massive amount of
graviton shear
. Such a phenomenon was experienced by the crew of the
USS
Voyager
in
2375
, when their vessel became trapped in a region of chaotic space in the
Delta Quadrant
. (
VOY
: "
The Fight
")

at
Wikipedia

A

because he was going too fast when Darem hit the eddy and then tried to stop. (

: "

")

. (

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravitational redshift
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravitational_redshift
======================================================================

Gravitational redshift
was the decrease in the
frequency
and
energy
and the increase in the
wavelength
of
electromagnetic waves
or
photons
travelling out of a
gravitational well
.
It was also an optical illusion that occurred as an object fell into a
black hole
. As the
speed
of the falling object exceeded the
frequency
of the
light
it emitted, to an outside observer it would appear to have stopped just outside the black hole. (
SNW
: "
Memento Mori
")
In the real world, the term "gravitational redshift" does not have this second definition.  Gravitational redshift is not an optical illusion and does not fit the phrase "it (the object falling into a black hole) would appear to have stopped just outside the black hole" in this second definition.  The phenomenon that does fit this phrase is called
gravitational time dilation
, but it too is not an illusion.
Speed and frequency are
dimensionally
different.  So, these two physical quantities cannot be compared directly.
If the object falls into the black hole and subsequently travels away faster than light, then the optical illusion is neither gravitational redshift nor gravitational time dilation, but the object appearing to be stopped just outside the black hole to an observer far from the black hole, when the object has actually already escaped the black hole by traveling faster than light.  However, on the one hand, due to gravitational redshift, any
electromagnetic radiation
going from the object to the observer will have frequency and energy approaching zero and wavelength approaching infinity such that the observer probably will not be able to see the object, and the illusion will be unseen. On the other hand,
faster-than-light radiation
can also escape the black hole, and any such radiation going from the object to the observer will give away the trick.
In
2259
,
Captain
Christopher Pike
took advantage of gravitational redshift to deceive a
Gorn destroyer
into believing that the
USS
Enterprise
had been destroyed, by accelerating toward the central black hole of the
Finibus system
while detonating an
AP 350
atmospheric processor
behind it.
Lieutenant
Erica Ortegas
termed this the "
Pike Maneuver
". (
SNW
: "
Memento Mori
")
In the real world, the Pike Maneuver can be described in the following manner: Pike took advantage of a combination of the block hole, gravitational time dilation, light (electromagnetic radiation), and
warp drive
to deceive the Gorn destroyer.  He would not have wanted to take advantage of gravitational redshift for the reason that at the black hole, this gravitational phenomenon would have redshifted the electromagnetic radiation to undetectability, rendering the illusion unobservable.  He would have had to offset it.  To do this, he would have had to exploit electromagnetic radiation with frequency and energy approaching infinity and wavelength approaching zero.  And because
subspace radiation
could travel faster than light, escape the black hole, and reach and alert the Gorn, he would have had to order
subspace silence
.
Furthermore, in exploiting this optical illusion, Pike would only have allowed the ship to linger close to the black hole just long enough for the ship to emit light to any observer far from the black hole. Because of gravitational time dilation, the longer the ship lingered, the further into the future - up to the end of the
Universe
- the ship would have traveled when it warped back to a distance far from the black hole.
External link
Gravitational redshift
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravitational slingshot
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravitational_slingshot
======================================================================

For the time travel method, please see
slingshot effect
.
The
gravitational slingshot
is a method of utilizing the gravitational pull of a large interstellar body as a means of propulsion. This technique is achieved by flying in a steep parabolic partial
orbit
around the body. It often appeared as if the object being propelled will crash into the body.
This technique was used in
2269
by
Captain
James T. Kirk
in order to fool a
malevolent entity
into leaving the
USS
Enterprise
. (
TAS
: "
Beyond the Farthest Star
")
It was also used in
2366
by Captain
Jean-Luc Picard
to escape a
booby-trapped
asteroid field
. (
TNG
: "
Booby Trap
")
External links
Gravitational slingshot
at
Memory Beta
, the wiki for licensed
Star Trek
works
Gravitational slingshot
at
Wikipedia

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravitational slipstream
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravitational_slipstream
======================================================================

Alternate reality
(
split 2233
)
Kirk and Krall caught in the gravitational slipstream of Yorktown
A
gravitational slipstream
was a "current" of force resulting from a balanced interaction of multiple
artificial gravity
fields. Such a slipstream was present at the central nexus of the
Federation
Starbase
Yorktown
.
In
2263
,
Captain
James T. Kirk
pursued
Krall
to the central nexus of Yorktown where Krall attempted to unleash the super weapon
Abronath
on the base's inhabitants.  Struggling within the starbase's
life support hub
, the two men were caught in the gravitational slipstream of Yorktown, causing them to fly around the exterior of
Yorktown Headquarters
. Krall was able to observe the path of the slipstream via the movement of broken glass within it, and use the slipstream to return himself to the hub. (
Star Trek Beyond
)

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravitational wave
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravitational_wave
======================================================================

Visualization of subspace gravitational waves produced by the Dark Matter Anomaly
A
gravitational wave
or
gravity wave
is a
gravitational
shift propagating across
space
. It carries
energy
as
gravitational radiation
.
The ancient
Promellians
harnessed gravity waves as an
energy source
. (
DIS
: "
Under the Twin Moons
")
In
2258
,
Starfleet
long-range sensors
detected high-energy
gamma rays
and gravitational waves consistent with a
quantum singularity
at the site of
USS
Discovery
's disappearance during the
battle with Control
. However, witnesses to the event all insisted that the ship exploded. (
DIS
: "
Such Sweet Sorrow, Part 2
")
In
2259
, while investigating a stable
vortex
on the
Kerkhovian moon
, the
shuttle
Cervantes
was overpowered by gravitational waves and collided with the
anomaly
. (
SNW
: "
Charades
")
In
3189
,
Zareh
detected high-energy gamma rays and gravitational waves preceding
Discovery
's appearance, which led him to conclude that they had
traveled through time
. (
DIS
: "
Far From Home
")
The
Dark Matter Anomaly
that appeared in
3190
generated
subspace
gravitational waves of extreme power, which were responsible for crippling
Deep Space Repair Beta Six
and destroying
Kwejian
. They were at first thought to be consistent with those produced by merging
binary black holes
; later close investigation by
Discovery
revealed the waves to have a different pattern. The waves damaged both
Discovery
and
Booker's ship
, which was able to "
surf
" one of the waves out of the DMA's
accretion disk
. (
DIS
: "
Anomaly (DIS)
")
Later that year, when the second DMA threatened
Earth
and
Ni'Var
,
debris
propelled by its gravitational waves reached both
planets
ahead of the anomaly itself. At Earth, the debris was accelerated to a
velocity
of 2,100
kilometers per second
. (
DIS
: "
The Galactic Barrier
", "
Coming Home
")
See also
Gravimetric wave
External link
Gravitational wave
at
Wikipedia

Display showing the graviton field output of the
USS
Enterprise

A
graviton field
is any area in which many
gravitons
may be found. Graviton fields are used in the production of
artificial gravity
. They are also found naturally-occurring in space.
Generally speaking, natural graviton fields appeared to be more powerful than man-made fields such as the one encountered by the
USS
Enterprise
-D
in
2367
. (
TNG
: "
The Loss
")
Later that year, the
Cytherian
-influenced
Reginald Barclay
modified the
Enterprise
nacelles
to create a highly charged graviton field, which created a
subspace distortion
and enabled the ship to travel to the Cytherian
homeworld
. (
TNG
: "
The Nth Degree
")
In
2369
, the graviton field of
Deep Space 9
's
tractor beam
was able to stabilize
Tosk
's
ship's
structural integrity
. (
DS9
: "
Captive Pursuit
")
Several weeks later, a
lifeform
from the
Gamma Quadrant
created a graviton field that drew DS9 towards the
wormhole
. (
DS9
: "
Q-Less
")
The graviton field output of the
shields
of the
Galaxy
-class
USS
Enterprise
-D
was 625
MCH
. (
Star Trek Generations
)
The
USS
Voyager
encountered a natural graviton field in
2373
. (
VOY
: "
Future's End
")
Lenara Kahn
and the
Trill Science Ministry
came up with a way to seal the
Bajoran wormhole
using a modulated graviton field. (
DS9
: "
In Purgatory's Shadow
")

PAGE: Graviton pulse
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Graviton_pulse

Multiple realities
(covers information from several
alternate timelines
)
A
graviton pulse
is a focused concentration of
graviton
particles
.
In
2368
, graviton pulses were used to attempt communication with the
Crystalline Entity
by the
USS
Enterprise
-D
. The Entity responded with its own graviton pulses, but an increased graviton pulse rate sent by
Dr.
Kila Marr
ultimately shattered the Entity. (
TNG
: "
Silicon Avatar
")
In
2369
, a coherent graviton pulse was used to close the
subspace
rupture that was allowing
solanogen-based lifeforms
into "normal"
space
. (
TNG
: "
Schisms
")
Also in 2369, a
Gamma Quadrant
artifact brought to
Deep Space 9
by
Vash
began to emit graviton pulses that disrupted station systems. The
space station
was dragged towards the
Bajoran wormhole
by the
gravity
created by the pulses, and received minor damage. (
DS9
: "
Q-Less
")
In an
alternate timeline
,
Benjamin Sisko
was hit by an
energy
discharge, which combined with a graviton pulse altered his temporal signature.
(
DS9
: "
The Visitor
")
In
2373
,
Arridor
and
Kol
, two
Ferengi
marooned in the
Delta Quadrant
as a result of the unstable
Barzan wormhole
, used a graviton pulse to prevent the
USS
Voyager
from transporting them off their
shuttle
. Subsequently, the pulse caused a
gravitational eddy
from the wormhole to pull the shuttle in and completely destabilized the wormhole itself. (
VOY
: "
False Profits
")
In
2375
, a graviton pulse was used by a small
Klingon
fleet to disrupt the
warp drives
of several pursuing
Jem'Hadar attack ships
. (
DS9
: "
Once More Unto the Breach
")
In
3191
,
Ensign
Adira Tal
told
Commander
Rayner
that a graviton pulse could be used to disrupt the
antimatter reactions
causing a
wormhole
to repeatedly open and close, but with a 43.7% chance of also causing an implosion that would seal it permanently. (
DIS
: "
Mirrors
")

======================================================================
PAGE: Gravity
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Gravity
======================================================================

For the
VOY
episode of the same name, please see "
Gravity
".
Kruge is pulled to his death by gravity
Gravity
(
g
) is one of the four main forces within the standard model of
particle
physics
. It has been
historically
defined as the
mass
between two objects. (
TOS
: "
Operation -- Annihilate!
") Gravity phenomena had a direct relationship to
field density
. (
TOS
: "
Requiem for Methuselah
")
Gravity was defined throughout the
universe
by a
gravitational constant
, which set the relative strength of the force. The
Q
had the ability to change the gravitational constant of the universe, and thereby redefine gravity. (
TNG
: "
Deja Q
")
Effects of gravity
While often considered an apocryphal story, the "invention" of physics, and a new era in the understanding of gravity was born the day the
apple
fell on
Isaac Newton
's
head
, thanks to the jostling of an apple
tree
by
Quinn
. (
TNG
: "
Descent
";
VOY
: "
Death Wish
")
Spock
once used a reference based on this "discovery" in a statement describing the behavior of
James T. Kirk
, stating, "
If I let go of a
hammer
on a
planet
that has a positive gravity, I need not see it fall to know that it has in fact fallen.
" (
TOS
: "
Court Martial
")
While
climbing
El Capitan
,
Spock
, using
levitation boots
, advised
Kirk
that he believed he didn't understand the gravity of the situation. But Kirk replied that "
gravity is foremost on my mind.
" (
Star Trek V: The Final Frontier
)
During a scan of
Aldean
DNA
,
Doctor
Beverly Crusher
was able to confirm that gravitational variations were not responsible for the Aldeans' sterility. (
TNG
: "
When The Bough Breaks
")
Earth normal
An
M class
planet was defined, in part, by having a gravity that was approximately equal to Earth's
sea level
. (
ENT
: "
Fallen Hero
") Gravity found to be similar to Earth was often described as "
Earth-normal
." (
TAS
: "
Beyond the Farthest Star
", "
The Eye of the Beholder
")
Other planets, such as
Talos IV
, had a gravity of 0.9
g
, which was ten percent "lighter" than the gravity found on Earth. (
TOS
: "
The Cage
", "
The Menagerie, Part I
") Contrarily,
Exo III
had a gravity of 1.1
g
, which was ten percent "heavier" than Earth's. (

: "

")
The gravity aboard the hulk of an abandoned
insectoid starship
was within two points of Earth-normal. (
TAS
: "

")
In the first draft

of
ENT
: "

Adaptations to gravity
Typically, the effects of gravity fluctuations on
humanoids
that are adapted to an "Earth-normal" gravity could cause them to get symptoms of
nausea
. (
DS9
: "
Treachery, Faith and the Great River
")
The manipulation of gravity, via means of
artificial gravity
, had been a scientific breakthrough for many
species
, dating back
billions of years
. (
TAS
: "
Beyond the Farthest Star
", "
The Slaver Weapon
")
Earth

technology
as early as the
22nd century
. (

: "

")
On more than one occasion, the gravity aboard the
USS
Enterprise
fell to 0.8
g
. (

: "

", "

") While this was not typical aboard Earth or

light on their feet. (

: "

") Captain

of the

's gravity at a level of 0.8

. (

While training a crew of former

. (

: "

")
Some

, which was capable of using gravity as a

. (

: "

")
Other species were capable of living in a variable-gravity environment, such as

. (

: "

")
The
Elaysians
were a humanoid species whose planet had a gravity much lower than that of Earth, and were unable to function fully in Earth-normal gravity. (

: "

")
When

to twenty

(

During the mid-

Multiple realities
(covers information from several
alternate timelines
)
Dyson sphere as viewed from the
Enterprise
bridge after entering its gravity well
A
gravity well
is a distortion of the
space-time continuum
caused by an object with
mass
, which can be conceptualized on a two-dimensional surface as a depression: the "well". The curvature of the well corresponds to
gravity
.
In
2155
in the
mirror universe
, the
Tholians
detonated a
tricobalt
warhead
in the gravity well of a dead star, which created an
interphasic rift
into another universe in the future of
2268
. (
ENT
: "
In A Mirror, Darkly
";
TOS
: "
The Tholian Web
")
In
2258
of the
alternate reality
, the
Constitution
-class
starship
USS
Enterprise
became caught in the gravity well of a
black hole
created by the explosion of a massive amount of
red matter
when the
Jellyfish
crashed into the
Narada
. Fortunately, the
Enterprise
managed to escape the gravity well after
Montgomery Scott
ejected the ship's multiple
warp cores
and detonated them, creating a large blast wave that pushed the ship out of danger. (
Star Trek
)
The
Bajoran wormhole
had its own gravity well. After a
carrier wave
emitted from the newly-established
wormhole relay station
created a
subspace inversion
in the
wormhole
in
2371
, its gravity well increased by a factor of three. (
DS9
: "
Destiny
")
In
2368
,
Wesley Crusher
and the
Nova Squadron
flew in a
diamond slot formation
around
Saturn
and came out of the gravity well of Saturn's
moon
Titan
, shortly before the Squadron suffered a catastrophic accident after attempting the dangerous maneuver
Kolvoord Starburst
, which claimed the life of
Joshua Albert
. (
TNG
: "
The First Duty
")
The
Dyson sphere
had an immense gravity well, not least due to the star at its center but the mass of the structure itself. As no radiant sunlight light or solar wind escaped from the sphere, starships were not able to detect the sphere until they were almost on top of it. As a result, the sphere's gravity well came as quite a shock to both the
USS
Jenolan
in
2294
and
USS
Enterprise
-D
in
2369
, so much so that the former was pulled in and crashed on the surface. (
TNG
: "
Relics
")
Later on, in a
holodeck
simulation, a holographic
James Moriarty
took control of the
Enterprise
-D and the ship became trapped in the gravity well of a
gas giant
in the
Detrian system
. To fool Moriarty into releasing the voice commands and regain command,
Jean-Luc Picard
created a holographic program,
Picard Delta One
to make Moriarty think he had left the
Enterprise
on the shuttlecraft
Sakharov
. (
TNG
: "
Ship In A Bottle
")
In 2369, two
quantum singularity lifeforms
came into this space-time continuum to save their
young
who were trapped in an artificial gravity well, the
engine core
of the
Romulan
warbird
. The aliens needed a natural gravity well to incubate their young and thought the engine core was a natural one. (
TNG
: "
Timescape
")
In
2370
,
Commander
Benjamin Sisko
ordered
Gideon Seyetik
to turn his
shuttlepod
around and return to the
USS
Prometheus
. Seyetik told Sisko that it was told late, as he had entered the gravity well of the dead star
Epsilon 119
. He later died after his shuttlepod crashed on Epsilon 119, but the star was re-ignited with the use of
protomatter
. (
DS9
: "
Second Sight
")
In
2374
,
Tuvok
and
Seven of Nine
were captured by the
Hirogen
. However, the ship they were on was slowly being pulled in by a
black hole
. On the
USS
Voyager
, the crew tried beaming them off but
Harry Kim
warned
Kathryn Janeway
that the gravity well from the black hole could scatter their patterns. Janeway saw no other choice and was ultimately successful in beaming them onto
Voyager
. (
VOY
: "
Hunters
")
It was also possible that while a planet may be found inside a rift that has the properties of a gravity well, the gravity on the planet's surface may be similar to Earth's.
Tom Paris
and
Tuvok
were stranded on such a planet while USS
Voyager
was nearly pulled inside a rift containing the planet in
2375
. Tuvok and Paris were later rescued. (
VOY
: "
Gravity
")
In
2381
, the
shuttlecraft
Yosemite
was damaged by
gravimetric shear
and caught in the gravity well of a nearby
desert planet
, causing it to
crash land
on the surface. (
LD
: "
Where Pleasant Fountains Lie
")
Later that year, the
USS
Archimedes
was caught in the gravity well of
Lapeeria
after being disabled by
magnetized ionic plasma
from an exploding
planetoid
. It almost crashed into the planet before it was saved by the
USS
Cerritos
. (
LD
: "
First First Contact
")
The USS
Protostar
being pulled into a white dwarf's gravity well
In
2383
, the
USS
Protostar
encountered a
binary star system
and was almost destroyed after being pulled into the gravity well of an orbiting
white dwarf
that was in the final moments of tearing apart its
red giant
companion, but was able to escape by riding the shockwave out of the gravity well's pull. (
PRO
: "

")

or

.

and
IV
were located in the

's habitable zone, and were marked as candidates for

when the

. (

: "

"
display graphic
)

's twelve planets was an uninhabited

PAGE: Hardness
CATEGORIES: Physics
URL: https://memory-alpha.fandom.com/wiki/Hardness
======================================================================

Hardness
was a measure of a
material
's resistance to certain types of deformation, such as indentation or abrasion. Inversely,
softness
was how easily those deformations could occur.
In
2266
,
Federation
Starfleet
officer
Spock
claimed that
cast
rodinium
was the hardest
substance
known
to their
science
. (
TOS
: "
Balance of Terror
")
In
2267
,
Captain
James T. Kirk
expressed uncertainty in
diamonds
being the hardest substance known in the
universe
. Spock later claimed that diamonds were the hardest known substance and thus would make formidable
projectiles
when impelled by the sufficient
force
of
gunpowder
. (
TOS
: "
Arena
")
In
2268
,
ermines
,
tribbles
, and
Regulan bloodworms
were described as soft. (
TOS
: "
The Trouble with Tribbles
")
That same year, Kirk stated that
pure
tritanium
was twenty times as hard as diamond, and Spock corrected him that it was exactly 21.4 times as hard. (
TOS
: "
Obsession
")
External link
Hardness
at
Wikipedia

The surface of the Praxillus star as it undergoes helium fusion enhancement.
Helium fusion enhancement
was a concept in which a dying
star
could be revitalized.
In
2367
, the
USS
Enterprise
-D
conducted a test on
Beta Praxillus
using specially-modified
photon torpedoes
, designed by
Kaelon
scientist
Timicin
. Due to the similarities of Beta Praxillus and the
Kaelon sun
, the test was designed to determine if the same process could be performed on the dying Kaelon sun, thereby saving the
Kaelon
. The photon torpedoes successfully reached Praxillus's
stellar core
, and at first it appeared that the experiment was successful. The star's temperature continued to increase, however, and the star
nova
. (
TNG
: "
Half a Life
")

Helium
Nuclear fusion

Multiple realities
(covers information from several
alternate timelines
)
Earth from high orbit
High orbit
, also known as
maximum orbit
or
extended orbit
, was the high
altitude
orbit
of an object above a
planetary body
, entirely above that of a
geosynchronous orbit
, or the orbital period exceeding the length of a
day
. For
Earth
, high orbit altitude was anything greater than 35,786
kilometers
.
Starships may maintain a large distance from the planet's surface for safety reasons but is still close enough to use the
transporter
. (
VOY
: "
Ex Post Facto
", "
The Omega Directive
")
The
USS
Voyager
assumed a high orbit over Earth, when it visited the planet in
1996
, at, according to
Rain Robinson
, an altitude of 20,000 kilometers. (
VOY
: "
Future's End
")
Twenty thousand kilometers is generally accepted as
medium Earth orbit
, specifically
semi-synchronous orbit
, where
Voyager
would have realistically orbited Earth once every twelve hours.
In anticipation of the blast from the detonation of
antimatter
used to kill the
dikironium cloud creature
on
Tycho IV
, the
USS
Enterprise
moved out to maximum orbit, holding at a range of 30,000 kilometers. (
TOS
: "
Obsession
")
After
time traveling
to
1968
Earth, the
Enterprise
used
deflector shields
to remain unobserved while in extended orbit. (
TOS
: "
Assignment: Earth
")
The
USS
Enterprise
-D
entered a high orbit over
Indri VIII
in
2369
. (
TNG
: "
The Chase
")
